The Anti-Slavery Society Convention of 1840 was held in London from June 12–23, organized by the British and Foreign Anti-Slavery Society. It aimed to promote the global abolition of slavery and protect emancipated 
populations. A pivotal moment arose when women delegates, including Lucretia Mott, were excluded from participating, galvanizing the U.S. women's suffrage movement. The event is immortalized in Benjamin Robert 
Haydon's painting *The Anti-Slavery Society Convention, 1840*, housed in the National Portrait Gallery.

The **Stadio Luigi Ferraris**, officially named **Stadio Comunale Luigi Ferraris**, is
a historic multi-use stadium in Genoa, Italy. Opened in **1911**, it is the oldest 
football stadium still in use in Italy and serves as the home ground for both **Genoa 
C.F.C.** and **U.C. Sampdoria**. Named after **Luigi Ferraris** (1887–1915), an 
Italian footballer and soldier who died in World War I, the stadium currently holds a 
capacity of **33,205** and has hosted major events, including Italy's 1949 match with 
Portugal (record attendance of 60,000). It is located in the Marassi neighborhood and 
is undergoing renovations for potential use in future tournaments like Euro 2032.

  }

  ages_at_release = {name: (boas_first_album_release_date - birthdate).days // 365    
  for name, birthdate in bts_members.items()}                                         
                                                                                      
  # Calculate the date when each member turned 5 years old                            
  turning_5_dates = {name: birthdate + datetime.timedelta(days=5*365) for name,       
  birthdate in bts_members.items()}                                                   
                                                                                      
  # Find the member who turned 5 the soonest after BoA's first album was released     
  soonest_turning_5 = min(turning_5_dates, key=lambda name: turning_5_dates[name] -   
  boas_first_album_release_date)

northern and central India, contributing significantly to the Gupta Empire's decline. 
By the early 6th century, they captured key regions like Punjab, Gujarat, and parts of
Madhya Pradesh, weakening Gupta authority. Though Emperor Skandagupta had earlier 
repelled a Huna invasion in the 5th century, the sustained Hunnic campaigns ultimately
led to the Gupta Empire's collapse by 550 CE.
